            <span class="t-bold mr1
                ">
              <span aria-hidden="true"><!---->Brazilian Derivatives and Securities - Pricing and Risk Management of FX and Interest-Rate Portfolios for Local and Global Markets<!----></span><span class="visually-hidden"><!---->Brazilian Derivatives and Securities - Pricing and Risk Management of FX and Interest-Rate Portfolios for Local and Global Markets<!----></span>
            </span>
<!----><!----><!---->        </div>
          <span class="t-14 t-normal">
            <span aria-hidden="true"><!---->Palgrave MacMillan · Mar 1, 2016<!----></span><span class="visually-hidden"><!---->Palgrave MacMillan · Mar 1, 2016<!----></span>

      <div class="pvs-list__outer-container">
<!---->    <ul class="pvs-list
        
        ">
        <li class=" ">
                      <div class="pv2">
              <a class="optional-action-target-wrapper artdeco-button artdeco-button--secondary artdeco-button--2 artdeco-button--muted 
      inline-flex justify-center align-self-flex-start
      
      " target="_blank" href="http://www.palgrave.com/page/detail/brazilian-derivatives-and-securities-/?isb=9781137477262">
<!---->      <span class="pvs-navigation__text">
        See publication
      </span>
  </a>


      </div>


        </li>
        <li class=" ">
                <div class="pvs-list__outer-container">
<!---->    <ul class="pvs-list
        
        ">
        <li class="pvs-list__item--with-top-padding ">
                <div class="display-flex ">
    <div class="display-flex full-width">
    
      
  <div class="pv-shared-text-with-see-more t-14 t-normal t-black display-flex align-items-center">
    <div class="inline-show-more-text
    inline-show-more-text--is-collapsed
    
    
    
    " style="line-height:1.9rem;max-height:3.8rem;">

    <span aria-hidden="true"><!---->The Brazilian financial markets operate in a very different way to their G7 counterparts. Key differences include onshore and offshore markets, exponential rates, business days day-counts and price formation from the futures markets (instead of the cash markets). Quants, traders, structurers and risk professionals active in this market need to understand these different dynamics in order to be able to effectively map these peculiarities into standard financial engineering techniques and work effectively.<!----><br><br><!---->Brazilian Derivatives and Securities is a quantitative, applied guide to the offshore and onshore Brazilian markets, with a focus on the financial instruments unique to the region. It offers a comprehensive introduction to the key financial ‘archaeology’ in the Brazil context, exploring interest rates, FX and inflation and key differences from G7 market finance. The book explores the dynamics of the local markets in detail, including cash instruments when necessary and provides valuable guidance on managing unique situations, from knowing what to do when the time series misbehaves, to how to distinguish volatility from structural changes.  Finally, the book introduces the region's unique financial instruments, as well as their pricing and risk management needs. Techniques for interpolation and consistency among different curves are described in detail, and heuristics for potential exposure calculations are developed.<!----><br><br><!---->Covering both introductory and complex topics, this book provides existing practitioners in Brazil, as well as those interested in becoming involved in these markets, everything they need to understand the market dynamics, risks, pricing and calibration of curves for all products currently available.<!----><br></span><span class="visually-hidden"><!---->The Brazilian financial markets operate in a very different way to their G7 counterparts. Key differences include onshore and offshore markets, exponential rates, business days day-counts and price formation from the futures markets (instead of the cash markets). Quants, traders, structurers and risk professionals active in this market need to understand these different dynamics in order to be able to effectively map these peculiarities into standard financial engineering techniques and work effectively.

Brazilian Derivatives and Securities is a quantitative, applied guide to the offshore and onshore Brazilian markets, with a focus on the financial instruments unique to the region. It offers a comprehensive introduction to the key financial ‘archaeology’ in the Brazil context, exploring interest rates, FX and inflation and key differences from G7 market finance. The book explores the dynamics of the local markets in detail, including cash instruments when necessary and provides valuable guidance on managing unique situations, from knowing what to do when the time series misbehaves, to how to distinguish volatility from structural changes.  Finally, the book introduces the region's unique financial instruments, as well as their pricing and risk management needs. Techniques for interpolation and consistency among different curves are described in detail, and heuristics for potential exposure calculations are developed.

Covering both introductory and complex topics, this book provides existing practitioners in Brazil, as well as those interested in becoming involved in these markets, everything they need to understand the market dynamics, risks, pricing and calibration of curves for all products currently available.<span class="white-space-pre"> </span></span>

<!----></div>
  </div>

  
  </div>
